Dear all,

	this is to confirm that I will attend the Darmstadt meeting. 
I will give a look at the relevant documentation in the next days, 
and I will try to offer some useful feedback in the light of the 
methodology we have developed here at LADSEB in the latest years.

	I will arrive in Darmstadt on Friday late evening (my flight 
arrives in Frankfurt at 18:55), maybe in time to join you somewhere. 
I will be lodging at the Maritim Konferenzhotel.

	See you soon,

From Koernig@ifs.tu-darmstadt.de  Tue Sep  4 07:56:45 2001
From: Koernig@ifs.tu-darmstadt.de (Stephan Koernig)
Date: Tue, 04 Sep 2001 08:56:45 +0200
Subject: [Cidoc-harmony-wg] Meeting in Darmstadt
Message-ID: <3B947B2D.BEED3AF1@ifs.tu-darmstadt.de>

Hi all,
please excuse my late answer on Martin's request for venue information.

Now here it comes...


The venue of our meeting will be the "Residenzschloss" (Building S3/13,
Marktplatz 15), in the city center not far away from the ECDL conference

venue

Have a look at http://www.soziologie.de/iuk2000/pics/map.jpg
(the venue marked as "Schloss", the trainstation is "Hauptbahnhof")

and at http://www.tu-darmstadt.de/lageplaene/darmstadt/stadtmitte/s3.tud

(where you can find Building S3/13)

>From the trainstation take Bus D direction "Ostbahnhof" or Bus F
direction "Oberwaldhaus" and get of at stop "Schloss", which is about a
7 minutes tour.

>From the ECDL conference venue it is even more convenient to take a bus

from bus stop "Berliner Alee". There you take the tram 9 or 10 in
direction "Böllenfalltor". Or take bus K direction Jaupstrasse, bus H
direction Parkstrasse or the two above mentioned busses.

In the building (Residenzschloss)  you have to find
"Institut fuer Soziologie/Philosophie" in the third floor.
The Roomnumber is 319. There will be
signs showing you the way.


Best wishes,
Stephan

Dear All,

Thank you very much for making this meeting a success. I have received
notes from Libby and Jane and will start creating consolidated minutes
from those. Particularly Libby's notes are a real treasure, so I am now
in the difficulty not to make a whole story out of it. Please do not hesitate
to send me more notes if you have any.

The next step will be for Harmony to create some example scenarios of
what a common model should be able to capture, in order to validate
potential modelling alternatives.

best wishes,

Martin
